[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethods:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `TraceDataFlowNativeCallbacks.traceCmpInt` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfuzzer instrumentation[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `RandomAccessReadBuffer.read`  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `BaseParser.skipSpaces` → `parseDirObject` → `parseCOSDictionaryValue` → [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`parseCOSDictionaryNameValuePair` → `parseCOSDictionary`  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `XrefParser.parseTrailer` → `XrefParser.parseXref` → [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`COSParser.retrieveTrailer` → `PDFParser.initialParse` → `PDFParser.parse`  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important observations:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • No other threads appear blocked or contending on locks—this is not a deadlock. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The parser is iterating through PDF structure elements [0m[1;39m([0m[39mspaces, dictionary [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentries, cross‐reference tables[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The harness merely feeds fuzzed bytes; the hang occurs within PDFBox internals.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Areas for investigation:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • PDFBox I/O layer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`RandomAccessReadBuffer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Base parsing logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`BaseParser` methods handling spaces and dictionary [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mobjects[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Cross‐reference parsing [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`XrefParser`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and trailer retrieval [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`COSParser`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Fuzzer instrumentation interactions via `TraceDataFlowNativeCallbacks`  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The way input boundaries and control flows are handled during parsing loops  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis report refrains from speculating on root causes or remediations and focuses on[0m [2m                [0m
